    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_2.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.y = exp2(u_xlat16_11);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = min(u_xlat16_2.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_20 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_20 + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_20);
    u_xlat16_2.xzw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xzw = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_2.xzw;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_2.y * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_11 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_11) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat18 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(u_xlat18) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xzw * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlatb0 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0;

    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;

    u_xlat16_28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_28);

    u_xlat16_28 = abs(u_xlat16_28) + 0.00400000019;

    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_29 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_29 = max(u_xlat16_29, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_29 = min(u_xlat16_29, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_29) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 6.0;

    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0);

    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_11;
    u_xlat16_11 = clamp(u_xlat16_11, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_20) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_29) + u_xlat16_20;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_29 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat16_20 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_20 = clamp(u_xlat16_20, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_4 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_11) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_14.xyz = (-u_xlat10_4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat10_4.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_20) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_14.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = clamp(u_xlat3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat12.x = (-u_xlat9.x) * u_xlat9.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat12.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat16_14.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat12.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat10_0.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat10_0.zzz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(vec3(_EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale));

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat0.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat0.xy = sin(u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_11 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat16_2.x + u_xlat16_11;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_2.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.y = exp2(u_xlat16_11);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = min(u_xlat16_2.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_20 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_20 + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_20);
    u_xlat16_2.xzw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xzw = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_2.xzw;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_2.y * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_11 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_11) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat18 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(u_xlat18) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xzw * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_ExtraTexture;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowPosition;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _flowFresnelPower;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowFresnelColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _flowFilp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_flowColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _PostUVFlip;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _FaceOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _ChangeFace;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmisssionColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _PortalPlane;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
float u_xlat11;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = in_POSITION0.z + (-_PortalPlane);
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

vec3 u_xlat0;

bool u_xlatb0;

void main()
{
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_28 = dot((-u_xlat9.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 + u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_28)) + (-u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = abs(u_xlat16_28) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_29 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_29 = max(u_xlat16_29, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_29 = min(u_xlat16_29, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_29) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(u_xlat16_2.x);

    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_29;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat9.xxx;
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_11) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_11;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_11 = min(max(u_xlat16_11, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

#endif
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_20) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_29) + u_xlat16_20;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_29 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat16_20 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_20 = min(max(u_xlat16_20, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_20 = clamp(u_xlat16_20, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_11) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_14.xyz = (-u_xlat16_4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_20) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_14.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9.x = min(max(u_xlat9.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat3.x = min(max(u_xlat3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat3.x = clamp(u_xlat3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat12.x = (-u_xlat9.x) * u_xlat9.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat12.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat16_14.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat12.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_0.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_0.zzz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(vec3(_EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_4.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat0.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat0.xy = sin(u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_11 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat16_2.x + u_xlat16_11;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_2.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.y = exp2(u_xlat16_11);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = min(u_xlat16_2.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_20 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_20 + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_20);
    u_xlat16_2.xzw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xzw * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;

    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_14.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = clamp(u_xlat3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat12.x = (-u_xlat9.x) * u_xlat9.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat12.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat16_14.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat12.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat10_0.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat10_0.zzz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(vec3(_EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_4.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat0.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat0.xy = sin(u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_11 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat16_2.x + u_xlat16_11;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_2.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.y = exp2(u_xlat16_11);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = min(u_xlat16_2.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_20 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_20 + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_20);
    u_xlat16_2.xzw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xzw = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_2.xzw;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_2.y * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_11 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_11) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat18 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(u_xlat18) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xzw * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = (-in_POSITION0.z) + _PortalPlane;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;

    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;

    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MouthTiling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MouthOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EyeTiling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EyeOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _AddTexST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddTexColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddTexScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_ExtraTexture;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowPosition;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _flowFresnelPower;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowFresnelColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _flowFilp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_flowColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _PostUVFlip;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _FaceOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _ChangeFace;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmisssionColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _PortalPlane;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
float u_xlat11;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = in_POSITION0.z + (-_PortalPlane);
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

vec3 u_xlat0;

bool u_xlatb0;

void main()
{
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_28 = dot((-u_xlat9.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 + u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_28)) + (-u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = abs(u_xlat16_28) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_29 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_29 = max(u_xlat16_29, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_29 = min(u_xlat16_29, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_29) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_29;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat9.xxx;
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_11) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_11;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_11 = min(max(u_xlat16_11, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_11 = clamp(u_xlat16_11, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_20) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_29) + u_xlat16_20;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_29 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat16_20 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_20 = min(max(u_xlat16_20, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_20 = clamp(u_xlat16_20, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_11) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_14.xyz = (-u_xlat16_4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_20) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_14.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat9.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9.x = min(max(u_xlat9.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat3.x = min(max(u_xlat3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat3.x = clamp(u_xlat3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat12.x = (-u_xlat9.x) * u_xlat9.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat12.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat16_14.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat12.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_0.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_0.zzz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(vec3(_EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_4.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat0.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat0.xy = sin(u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_11 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_11) + u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat16_2.x + u_xlat16_11;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;

    u_xlat0.xy = sin(u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_17.x = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_17.x) + u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat16_6.x + u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xxx;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_1.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = log2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_6.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_6.x = exp2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.y = exp2(u_xlat16_17.x);
    u_xlat16_6.xy = min(u_xlat16_6.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_28 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_28 + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_6.xy = u_xlat16_6.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_6.xzw = u_xlat16_6.xxx * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xzw = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_6.xzw;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_6.y * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_17.x * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_17.xxx * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat22 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(u_xlat22) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17.x = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_17.xxx + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xzw * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_34) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

#else

#endif

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = (-in_POSITION0.x) + _PortalPlane;
    u_xlat5 = in_POSITION0.x + _PortalPlane;
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat5) + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = _PostUVFlip * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat5;

    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;

in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;

bool u_xlatb30;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
mediump float u_xlat16_33;
void main()
{
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w * u_xlat16_1.x;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb30 = !!(u_xlat2.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb30 = u_xlat2.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb30){discard;}
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = max(u_xlat30, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat30) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_31)) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = abs(u_xlat16_31) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_2.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_33 = max(u_xlat16_33, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_33 = min(u_xlat16_33, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_33) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_5.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat30 = float(1.0) / u_xlat30;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat30 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat30 * u_xlat30;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_2.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_23 = (-u_xlat16_13) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_13;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_13 = min(max(u_xlat16_13, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_13 = clamp(u_xlat16_13, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_23 = (-u_xlat16_23) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_23 = (-u_xlat16_33) + u_xlat16_23;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_33 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_23 = u_xlat16_23 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_23 = min(max(u_xlat16_23, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_23 = clamp(u_xlat16_23, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_13) * u_xlat8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_13) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_23) + (-u_xlat8.xyz);

    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_16.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = clamp(u_xlat12, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat4.x = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat4.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_6.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat30 * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat30 = min(u_xlat30, 100.0);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = min(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_2.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat10_2.zzz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(vec3(_EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale, _EmisssionScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat0.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat0.xy = sin(u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_13 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat16_13) + u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat16_3.x + u_xlat16_13;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_3.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.y = exp2(u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = min(u_xlat16_3.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_23 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_23 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_23 + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_23);
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_3.y * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_13 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_13) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat20 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(u_xlat20) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_13) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xzw * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = (-in_POSITION0.x) + _PortalPlane;

    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);

    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlatb0 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff0);

    u_xlatb30 = !!(u_xlat2.x<0.0);
#else

#endif

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;

    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;

    u_xlat30 = max(u_xlat30, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_31)) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_31 = max(u_xlat16_31, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * 6.0;

    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);

    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35 + 1.0;
    u_xlat30 = float(1.0) / u_xlat30;

#else

#endif
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_15) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_31 = (-u_xlat16_31) + u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_31 = min(max(u_xlat16_31, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_31 = clamp(u_xlat16_31, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * u_xlat16_5.xxx + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = abs(u_xlat16_31) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);
    u_xlat30 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat30 * u_xlat30;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_35) * u_xlat8.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = (-u_xlat2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat2.zxy) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = (-u_xlat2.zxy) * u_xlat7.yzx;
    u_xlat8.xyz = (-u_xlat2.yzx) * u_xlat7.zxy + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat7.z = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat7.y = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat30 = min(max(u_xlat30, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat30 = clamp(u_xlat30, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(u_xlat30) * u_xlat7.xy;
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat2.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat2.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = min(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat0.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat0.xy = sin(u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_15 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_15) + u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat16_5.x + u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_5.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);

    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.y = exp2(u_xlat16_15);

    u_xlat16_25 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_25 + _DOTEmissionMax;

    u_xlat20 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(u_xlat20) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat0.xy;

    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_15) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;

    u_xlat16_31 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);

    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightIndices[2];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BumpMap_ST;

	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _FaceOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _ChangeFace;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmisssionColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _PortalPlane;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat5;
float u_xlat6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
float u_xlat11;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = (-in_POSITION0.x) + _PortalPlane;
    u_xlat5 = in_POSITION0.x + _PortalPlane;
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat5) + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = _PostUVFlip * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat5;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _AdditionalTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
float u_xlat20;
mediump float u_xlat16_25;
float u_xlat30;
bool u_xlatb30;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
mediump float u_xlat16_33;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w * u_xlat16_1.x;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb30 = !!(u_xlat2.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb30 = u_xlat2.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb30){discard;}
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = max(u_xlat30, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_31)) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_31 = max(u_xlat16_31, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_33 = (-u_xlat16_31) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_3 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35 + 1.0;
    u_xlat30 = float(1.0) / u_xlat30;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_5.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_5.x = min(max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_5.x = clamp(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_15) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_31 = (-u_xlat16_31) + u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_31 = min(max(u_xlat16_31, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_31 = clamp(u_xlat16_31, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * u_xlat16_5.xxx + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = abs(u_xlat16_31) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);
    u_xlat30 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat30 * u_xlat30;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_35) * u_xlat8.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = (-u_xlat2.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat2.zxy) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = (-u_xlat2.zxy) * u_xlat7.yzx;
    u_xlat8.xyz = (-u_xlat2.yzx) * u_xlat7.zxy + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat7.z = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat30);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat7.y = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat30 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);

    u_xlat30 = min(max(u_xlat30, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat30 = clamp(u_xlat30, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat2 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat2 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat1.w;
    gl_Position.z = (-u_xlat0.x) + u_xlat1.z;
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw;
    u_xlat0.w = (-in_POSITION0.z) + _PortalPlane;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

    precision highp float;
#else
    precision mediump float;
#endif

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat2;

vec3 u_xlat3;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_COLOR0.w);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + in_COLOR0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) * 0.0500000007 + -0.100000001;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, in_NORMAL0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat3.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(0.0250000004, 0.0250000004, 0.0250000004) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat3.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat3.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat3.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat2 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat1.w;
    gl_Position.z = (-u_xlat0.x) + u_xlat1.z;
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw;
    u_xlat0.w = in_POSITION0.z + (-_PortalPlane);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

precision highp int;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3

#else

#endif

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
